Row-level `tenant_id` columns are only present on master DB tables (tenants, tenant_usage, billing); per-tenant tables don't need them. No code change; documented as verified.

- [x] PROD55. `services/backup.ts` forces `shouldEncrypt = true` when `config.nodeEnv === 'production'`, overriding the admin-toggleable `backup_encrypt` flag and any opts.encrypt override. Only `.db.enc` artifacts land under backup_path in production; encryptFile() already unlinks the plaintext input. Dev retains the opt-in behavior for engineer convenience. Commit 3ac65b4.

- [x] PROD54. `services/backup.ts:getPassphrase()` throws `BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY is required in production. ... refusing to encrypt with JWT_SECRET fallback.` when `config.nodeEnv === 'production'` and the key is missing. Previously silently fell back to JWT_SECRET with a warn log ŌåÆ any JWT rotation bricked every backup. Dev retains the warning-only fallback so self-hosted test installs work without a dedicated key. Commit 9342fa7.

- [x] PROD46. Master DB backups encrypted with `BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY` ŌĆö same encryptFile() path is now hard-gated in production (see PROD54). Closes with commit 9342fa7.

- [x] PROD52. Correlation ID middleware in `index.ts` (mounted right after the HTTPS redirect, before helmet/cors) attaches `res.locals.requestId` and echoes `X-Request-Id` on every response. Prefers validated-incoming header `[A-Za-z0-9_.:+-]{1,128}` for cross-service log chaining; falls back to `crypto.randomUUID()`. Hostile incoming values with CRLF/log-separator chars rejected ŌåÆ fresh UUID. Enables "paste the reference from the user's error screen into the log aggregator" support flow. Commit eb4a9fe.

- [x] PROD29. New `utils/ssrfGuard.ts` exports `assertPublicUrl(url)` + `fetchWithSsrfGuard`. Blocks non-http(s) schemes + every resolved IP in private/reserved ranges (RFC 1918, 127/8, 169.254/16 inc. AWS IMDS, 100.64/10 CGNAT, multicast, reserved; IPv6 ::1, fc00::/7, fe80::/10, IPv4-mapped). DNS lookup requests ALL addresses and rejects if ANY is private ŌåÆ closes rebinding. Applied to `services/webhooks.ts attemptDelivery()` and `services/catalogScraper.ts fetchSearchPage()`. `githubUpdater.ts` uses child-process `git fetch` (no HTTP fetch; covered by origin-URL whitelist). Commits a5a3b56 + dd83f4d.

- [x] SEC-H20-partial. Super-admin JWT `expiresIn` shortened from `4h` to `30m` (`super-admin.routes.ts:19`). Full-fleet mutation blast radius too large for a 4h window ŌĆö 30m aligns with PCI-DSS privileged-access guidance. Step-up TOTP on destructive endpoints (the remainder of SEC-H20) tracked as follow-up since it needs a UI prompt path. Commit b0ae99e.

- [x] SEC-M17. `tradeIns.routes.ts` PATCH `/:id` ŌĆö accepting a trade-in now commits an inventory row and store credit atomically with the status flip. Previously the handler only updated `trade_ins` and left inventory + store credit to separate follow-up calls that could silently never run (or run twice, or run after a crash). New flow: pull existing `status, customer_id, device_name, condition, accepted_price` up front; detect the "was-not-accepted ŌåÆ is-now-accepted AND effective accepted_price > 0" transition, build a `TxQuery[]` batch containing (a) the UPDATE on trade_ins, (b) an INSERT into inventory_items (name=device_name, item_type='product', device_type='trade_in:<condition>', cost/retail=accepted_price, in_stock=1, is_active=1), (c) store_credits balance upsert (read-then-branch because 026_refunds_credits.sql has no UNIQUE(customer_id) ŌĆö falls back to UPDATE if the row exists, INSERT if not), (d) store_credit_transactions ledger row (`type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='trade_in'`, `reference_id=trade_in_id`, `notes='Trade-in credit'`). Inventory INSERT always runs on accept (simplest path); store credit only mints when customer_id is set (null customer_id is a valid state for walk-in / one-off trade-ins, ledger stays clean). Audit entry grows `accepted_transition` + `store_credit_issued` fields. Commit bdab160.

- [x] SEC-L18. `index.ts` ŌĆö new per-tenant failure circuit wraps the tenant-retention-sweep (hourlyŌåÆdaily at 02:00 local) and appointment-reminder (every 15 min) cron handlers. One bad tenant (corrupt DB, schema drift, wedged SMS provider) used to burn CPU on every subsequent tick forever ŌĆö the inner try/catch swallowed errors but the same doomed code path re-ran every tick. Added `cronCircuits: Map<string, {consecutiveFailures, openUntil}>` alongside the existing `cronLastRun` map, with helpers `circuitAllowsRun`, `recordCircuitFailure`, `recordCircuitSuccess` keyed on `(cronName, tenantSlug ?? 'default')`. After 5 consecutive failures the tenant is skipped for 10 minutes before retrying; any success clears the counter and the open window both. For appointment reminders, a per-message SMS failure does NOT count as a tenant-level failure (bad phone numbers and transient provider errors are bounded by design); only an uncaught tenant-work failure rolls up. Circuit state is in-memory per-process ŌĆö cron jobs only run on one node so this is fine. Commit 4414d5c.

- [x] SEC-M43. `pos.routes.ts` `/checkout-with-ticket` ŌĆö card-method overpayment now routes excess to store credit instead of silently dropping it. Previously `change = max(0, paid - total)` fired on every payment method, including card. On cash that's correct (hand back a bill); on card BlockChyp had charged the full amount but the invoice clamped amount_paid to total and the rest evaporated. New flow: card tenders (`card`, `credit`, `debit`, `blockchyp`, `stripe`) get their overpayment captured into `cardOverpayment`; in split-payment mode, cash tenders first cover the invoice total and only the card-method excess is store-credited (prevents mixed $50 cash + $100 card on a $90 invoice from losing the card excess). All payment inserts + POS transaction insert + store_credits upsert + store_credit_transactions ledger INSERT now build a `TxQuery[]` batch and run under one `adb.transaction()`. store_credits upsert uses the same read-then-branch pattern as SEC-M17. Ledger fields: `type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='card_overpayment'`, `reference_id=invoice_id`, notes identifying the method. Response now exposes `store_credit_issued` so the UI can show the split instead of silently pocketing. Commit 1c0f73a.

- [x] SEC-M44. New migration `100_payment_capture_state.sql` adds a `capture_state TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'captured' CHECK (capture_state IN ('authorized','captured','voided'))` column to `payments` plus an index on that column. Backfills defensively (`UPDATE payments SET capture_state = 'captured' WHERE capture_state IS NULL`). `refunds.routes.ts` POST `/` now rejects with 400 when any payment on the target invoice has `capture_state != 'captured'` ŌĆö blocks refunding money that was never captured (auth-only) or already released (voided). Error message names the count and the distinct non-captured states so the operator knows whether to capture or void first. Uses `COALESCE(capture_state, 'captured')` for defense-in-depth against any row that somehow escapes the backfill. `blockchyp.routes.ts` charge INSERT now writes `capture_state='captured'` explicitly since BlockChyp charges capture immediately on approval; making it explicit removes the silent dependency on the column default. Stripe INSERT sites: none currently exist server-side (Stripe flows today go through webhook paths that don't insert into payments); default 'captured' covers any future direct INSERTs. Commit 1fe0f60.

- [x] SEC-M51. `auth.routes.ts` TOTP encryption key derivation ŌĆö v3 replaces raw `SHA-256(jwt+sa)` with HKDF-based (RFC 5869) derivation using `crypto.hkdfSync('sha256', Buffer.from(jwt+sa), Buffer.from('bizarre-totp-salt-v3'), Buffer.from('totp-key-v3'), 32)` and binds the version tag as AES-GCM AAD via `cipher.setAAD(Buffer.from('v3'))`. HKDF's extract/expand pattern gives a proper PRF with salt injection and `info`/IKM/salt domain separation; raw SHA-256 over a concatenated string provides none of that. AAD binding closes a theoretical downgrade-by-prefix-rewrite: tampering the version prefix on `v3:iv:tag:data` now fails the GCM auth tag (verified manually ŌĆö rewriting v3ŌåÆv4 fails with `Unsupported state or unable to authenticate data`). v1/v2 legacy keys stay in `ENCRYPTION_KEYS` for decrypt; `decryptSecret` only calls `setAAD` when `version >= 3` so all pre-existing ciphertexts continue to read unchanged. New encrypts route through `CURRENT_KEY_VERSION=3`. `super-admin.routes.ts:94,103` is still using the old `sha256(sa + ':totp:superadmin')` pattern ŌĆö separate follow-up; out of scope for this commit. Commit e85a2e1.

- [x] SEC-H18. `middleware/auth.ts:185` `requirePermission()` evaluation order flipped: customRolePermissions now runs BEFORE the `users.role === 'admin'` bypass. Previously an admin assigned a narrow custom role via `PUT /roles/users/:userId/role` (which writes `user_custom_roles` only, not `users.role`) kept full permissions because the admin bypass short-circuited. Now the custom role is authoritative when assigned; legacy admin bypass still applies when no custom role is pinned (prevents org lockout). Commit 2a99b6b.

- [x] CROSS38b-notif. Android Settings > Notifications preferences sub-page. New `NotificationSettingsScreen.kt` (VM + Composable) wired via a new `Screen.NotificationSettings` route (`settings/notifications`). Six toggle rows split across two cards: Delivery channels (Email alerts / SMS alerts / Push notifications) and Categories (Low-stock / New-ticket / Appointment-reminder). Each backed by a new boolean on `AppPreferences` (`notifEmailAlertsEnabled`, `notifSmsAlertsEnabled`, `notifPushEnabled`, `notifLowStockEnabled`, `notifNewTicketEnabled`, `notifAppointmentReminderEnabled`) defaulting ON. `SettingsScreen` gains a new `onNotificationSettings: (() -> Unit)?` callback and renders a top-level "Notifications" `SettingsRow` using the same card-with-clickable-row shape as Edit Profile, sitting under SETTINGS. `AppNavGraph` registers the route, the SettingsScreen composable passes `onNotificationSettings = { navController.navigate(Screen.NotificationSettings.route) }`, and the NotificationSettings composable pops back on its own back button. Distinct from the notifications INBOX (`NotificationListScreen`) per CROSS54 ŌĆö this configures which events fire; the inbox lists events that already fired.

- [x] PROD12. Migration 101_pin_set_flag.sql adds `users.pin_set INTEGER DEFAULT 0`. `/auth/switch-user` rejects with 403 + `code: 'PIN_NOT_SET'` when matched user's pin_set is 0 (still on provisioning default '1234'). `/auth/change-pin` flips pin_set ŌåÆ 1 on success. Mirrors password_set flow. Existing users forced to rotate on next switch ŌĆö safer default than silently accepting 1234. Commit fceebbe.

- [x] PROD32. `index.ts` ŌĆö HSTS header now only emitted in production via a `hstsConfig` constant (`config.nodeEnv === 'production' ? { maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true } : false`). Prior config sent `max-age=63072000; includeSubDomains; preload` unconditionally, which burned the self-signed dev cert into every local browser cache and required a manual `chrome://net-internals/#hsts` purge on a fresh checkout. 180-day max-age matches the TODO.md spec and gives operators a reasonable rotation window without locking clients out on a cert swap. `preload` intentionally omitted ŌĆö hstspreload.org registration is a separate opt-in decision once the operator controls a real apex cert. Commit c145c7f.

- [x] PROD33. Audit of all 5 `res.cookie()` call sites in `packages/server/src`: `auth.routes.ts:271` (refreshToken on login), `:828` (deviceTrust), `:1024` (refresh rotation), `:1179` (impersonation), and `utils/csrf.ts:32` (portalCsrfToken). All had `HttpOnly` (except CSRF intentionally JS-readable for the double-submit pattern) and `SameSite` already set ŌĆö but `Secure` was hardcoded `true`, which silently drops the cookie on any dev tooling that talks plain HTTP. Gated `Secure` on `config.nodeEnv === 'production'` on all five so prod still forces HTTPS-only cookies while dev over HTTP (test tablets / curl) gets a usable session. No change to HttpOnly/SameSite/path/maxAge semantics. Auth cookies keep `SameSite=strict`; CSRF keeps `SameSite=lax` + `httpOnly=false` per double-submit design. Commit f706cbf.

- [x] PROD34. `index.ts` helmet CSP audit ŌĆö docs-only outcome, already tight. Global CSP: `default-src 'self'`, `script-src 'self' https://static.cloudflareinsights.com` (NO `'unsafe-inline'` in global CSP for prod OR dev ŌĆö Vite HMR uses `<script src=>` + eventsource, not inline), `script-src-attr 'self'` (no inline onclick handlers), `frame-ancestors 'none'` globally with per-tenant allowlist on `/widget`. `style-src 'unsafe-inline'` retained intentionally ŌĆö Tailwind runtime utilities and React-injected `<style>` tags require it; style-injection blast radius is far smaller than script injection. Documented exceptions: `/admin` and `/super-admin` HTML routes set a relaxed per-route CSP with script `'unsafe-inline'` for legacy inline onclick handlers in the backup panel ŌĆö both routes are localhost-only, scoped override not a global relaxation. Added PROD34 block comment above global `helmet()` call and expanded comment on `adminCsp` constant so a future auditor doesn't re-derive what's tight vs. relaxed. Commit c3738a7.

- [x] PROD36. `index.ts:799-856` CORS config audit + harden. Prior inline origin callback mixed the no-origin fast path with the allowlist match, making it easy for a future refactor to accidentally short-circuit and reflect an unvetted origin while `credentials: true` is set (the classic CORS-spec violation). Extracted the match into `isCorsOriginAllowed(origin)` so the rule is: no Origin -> `callback(null, true)` (no ACAO emitted anyway, credentials moot); origin in allowedOrigins / BASE_DOMAIN + subdomains / LAN (dev only) -> reflect; anything else -> reject with `new Error('CORS not allowed')`. Added PROD36 comment block making explicit that credentials can only ride on a reflected explicit origin, never on `*`. No behavior change for legitimate clients; hardens against future refactor drift. Commit b2ca864.

- [x] PROD37. `ws/server.ts` WebSocket upgrade audit. Existing protections verified: `index.ts:670-685` `verifyClient` rejects bad Origin with 403 BEFORE socket accept (SEC-WS1, mirrors HTTP CORS allowlist); 5-second `authTimeoutHandle` terminates any socket that has not sent a valid `{type:'auth', token}` frame; invalid JWT closes with 1008 + clears timer; per-socket 60/min rate limit closes with 1008. Gap closed: an unauthenticated socket that sent a non-auth message used to log a warning, reply with an `error` frame, and leave the socket open for the full 5s window ŌĆö a scanner could hold sockets open and burn fd + heap. Now `close(1008, 'not authenticated')` fires on the first non-auth inbound, shrinking the window from 5s to one message round-trip. Token-at-handshake (query param / subprotocol) kept out of scope ŌĆö browser WebSocket constructor cannot set custom headers, and moving the check earlier would require concurrent web + Android client rewrites. Commit bb191b9.

Each row is `T-XXXXX (mono) ┬Ę device name ┬Ę BrandStatusBadge ┬Ę $price`, tap routes to `TicketDetail` via the existing `onNavigateToTicket` callback. - [x] SEC-H19. `startAutoClockoutSweep` in `employees.routes.ts:618` now iterates every active tenant DB in multi-tenant mode instead of running once against `config.dbPath` (which points at master in MT). Per-tenant errors log + skip so one broken DB doesn't block the rest. Before: every tenant's stale clock entries stayed open forever. Commit 70c0325.

- [x] SEC-H17. Closes the vector where an attacker with a stolen backup code + leaked email could run recovery and immediately escalate / demote other admins before the real user notices. Password/PIN change within the window still allowed. Commit 8d90bfc.

- [x] NEW-TLIST-GRP. Android ticket list rows now render a small group pill to the LEFT of the specific status badge so the high-level bucket is scannable at a glance. Rendered as a compact `Surface` pill (`surfaceVariant` bg + single-hue label text) matching the `BrandStatusBadge` visual weight, with a 6dp spacer between the group pill and the specific status badge. Non-breaking for the existing trailing-column layout (pill + badge live in a nested `Row`, the money line stays on the second line). Because `TicketEntity` does not carry a dedicated `is_cancelled` column (only `statusIsClosed`), cancellation is inferred from the status-name heuristic ŌĆö same style the spec already allowed for the Waiting group.

- [x] SEC-H33. Payment-link public routes verified as DB-level tenant-isolated: `payment_links` has no `tenant_id` column because the architecture uses a per-tenant SQLite file. Global `tenantResolver` middleware (`index.ts:967`) rewrites `req.asyncDb` to the per-tenant DB based on Host subdomain, so a token minted in tenant A's file cannot be found via tenant B's Host. - [x] SEC-H24. `tracking.routes.ts:77` `toPublicTicket()` no longer includes `tracking_token` in the unauth `/track/:orderId` response. Token is a 32-char random bearer credential ŌĆö returning it in a public lookup let any probe with a valid order_id harvest the token and reuse it on other portal paths to impersonate the customer. Authenticated `/customers/:id/tickets` still returns it (role-gated). SMS-OTP-gated reveal remains future work. Commit e4fc965.

- [x] SEC-M60. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` ŌĆö `/:token/click` and `/:token/pay` now reject with 410 Gone when `expires_at` is in the past. Prior code only enforced `status = 'active'` which left active-but-stale rows replayable until someone hit GET (which is the only handler that auto-flipped `status` to `'expired'`). Both mutation endpoints now SELECT `expires_at` alongside the row, flip to `'expired'` when the check fires, and throw `new AppError('Payment link has expired', 410)`. Portal UI can read 410 as "permanently unavailable ŌĆö ask shop for a new link" instead of treating it like a transient failure.

- [x] SEC-M45. Portal `portalAuth` middleware now enforces a 4-hour idle timeout on top of the existing 24-hour absolute `expires_at`. Pulls `last_used_at` on lookup; if stale, DELETEs the session row and returns 401 `Session idle timeout. Please log in again.` Active users (who touch `last_used_at` every request) never kicked. Closes the shared-workstation resume-as-previous-customer vector. CSRF synchronizer-token migration out of scope this pass ŌĆö separate work. Commit c1f8dc9.

- [x] SEC-M59. `estimates.routes.ts:893-926` ŌĆö NULL `approval_token_expires_at` no longer means "never expires". Previously the expiry branch was gated on truthy check which silently skipped enforcement for legacy rows signed before the expiry-policy migration, leaving leaked pre-policy links replayable indefinitely. Now the code explicitly rejects with 410 Gone (`"Estimate approval token has no expiry ŌĆö signed before expiry policy rolled out; ask shop to reissue"`) so the shop has to reissue the estimate. The 410 status (vs 403) tells email clients / portal UI the resource is permanently unavailable so UX can render a clear "ask for a fresh link" message instead of looking like a generic auth failure.

- [x] SEC-M50. `db/tenant-pool.ts:104` ŌĆö no code change. `busy_timeout = 5000` was already correct. Added a rationale comment documenting the choice: multiple crons (session cleanup, payment-idempotency janitor, retention sweeps, appointment reminder) race on the same tenant DB when tick intervals overlap, and the 5s window serializes writers instead of letting SQLite return `SQLITE_BUSY` immediately. 5s covers normal DELETE / WAL checkpoint + safety, short enough that a genuinely stuck writer is surfaced rather than papered over for minutes. Raising this would mask real deadlocks; lowering causes flaky retention runs on busy tenants.

- [x] SEC-M54. `/estimates/bulk-convert` now refunds unused quota slots via `UPDATE tenant_usage SET tickets_created = MAX(0, tickets_created - failCount)` after the conversion loop. Prior flow atomically reserved `estimateCount` up-front and kept every slot even if mid-loop failures (not-found / already-converted) left fewer real tickets created ŌĆö permanent over-charge against monthly plan limit. Best-effort refund: master DB failures log without throwing, so the user's mixed-result response isn't replaced by a 500. Runs only on multi-tenant + finite tier. Commit b9c0db7.

- [x] SEC-M49. `index.ts` ŌĆö new daily per-tenant DB size observability cron. Fires once per UTC day during hour 02 (between the 02:00 tenant-timezone retention sweeps and the 03:00 master retention sweep), guarded by `shouldRunDaily('tenant-db-size-monitor', 'UTC')` so it runs exactly once even if the hourly interval lands multiple times in the window. Per tenant, it reads `tenantDb.name` (the better-sqlite3 file path), calls `fs.statSync(dbFile).size`, and emits one `log.info('tenant db size', { slug, sizeBytes, sizeMB })`. No archival, no delete ŌĆö that belongs to SEC-AL5 (audit logs) and the retention sweeper respectively. One syscall per tenant per day, negligible budget. Ops can chart DB growth over time and catch a runaway tenant before it stalls the whole node on a full disk.

Failures log warn and archive proceeds ŌĆö dead tenant shouldn't hang on Stripe 5xx. Closes PII-retention gap on archive. Commit fa72b3c.

- [x] SEC-M56. `sms.routes.ts` ŌĆö two-part hardening. (1) Per-destination rate limit: before inserting the outbound row we call `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'sms_per_destination', convPhone, 3, 3600_000)` so at most 3 messages/hour can be sent to the same normalized phone number. Keyed on `convPhone` so "+15551234567" and "(555) 123-4567" hit the same counter. Prevents buggy integrations / template-render loops from hammering one customer with dozens of messages in a few minutes. (2) Phone redaction in logs: new `redactPhone()` helper masks the carrier prefix and keeps only last 4 (`XXX-XXX-4567`). Applied to `logger.warn('outbound sms not delivered', { to, ... })` -> `{ toRedacted, ... }` and `logger.info('sms auto-reply sent off-hours', { from })` -> `{ fromRedacted }`. Customer phone numbers no longer land unredacted in the ops log aggregator / shared dashboard.

- [x] SEC-M58. `services/dunningScheduler.ts:408` `cutoffDateIso()` now takes a `timeZone` param; callsite reads `store_config.store_timezone` via new `getTenantTimezone()` helper. Uses `Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone })` for clean YYYY-MM-DD in tenant zone. Prior UTC cutoff produced 7h early/late drift on non-UTC tenants around DST, causing embarrassing 11 PM SMS sends. No new deps. Commit 6e9268c.

- [x] SEC-M55. `sms.routes.ts:414-440` ŌĆö POST `/sms/send` now enforces a per-tenant daily outbound cap in addition to the existing 5/min per-user window limiter. Before inserting the outbound row we run `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sms_messages WHERE direction='outbound' AND status NOT IN ('failed','simulated') AND created_at > datetime('now','-1 day')` and throw a 429 once the count hits `DAILY_TENANT_SMS_CAP` (default 500, override via env `TENANT_SMS_DAILY_CAP`). `'sending'` and `'scheduled'` rows are included in the count so in-flight messages debit the ceiling and a burst cannot race past the limit before statuses settle. Carrier-fraud containment: bounds a compromised tenant / stolen API token to at most 500 messages/day instead of 7200 (what the 5/min limiter allows at steady drip).

- [x] SEC-M41. Migration 099 adds `user_id` column to `payment_idempotency` + new `UNIQUE(invoice_id, client_request_id, user_id)`. `blockchyp.routes.ts:178` lookup + reserve INSERT now include `req.user!.id`. Prior narrow UNIQUE let a stolen `(invoice_id, idempotency_key)` pair replay from another user's session and leak original charge's transaction_id/amount via the 'replayed' happy path. Existing rows backfilled from `invoices.created_by`. Commit 8e727cd.

- [x] SEC-M52. `index.ts:792-817` production CORS no longer auto-accepts RFC1918 / CGNAT / localhost origins. The LAN / loopback regex now runs only when `config.nodeEnv !== 'production'` so prod is narrowed to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` + `BASE_DOMAIN` (+ subdomains). Dev retains the permissive rule so shop tablets can hit the server by LAN IP during testing. If an operator wants to whitelist a LAN origin in prod they must add it explicitly to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` in the env. Closes the browser-extension / shared-host spoof path where a malicious neighbor on the LAN forges an `Origin: http://192.168.x.x` to bypass CORS against the public API.

- [x] SEC-M37. `inventory.routes.ts:1680` quick-add now runs `cost_price` / `retail_price` through `validatePrice()` (400 on non-finite / negative); empty/undefined still defaults to 0 for the convenience flow. `repairPricing.routes.ts:45-46` gains a local `safeNum()` wrapping `parseFloat` + `Number.isFinite` check when reading `repair_price_flat_adjustment` / `repair_price_pct_adjustment` from `store_config` so bad rows can't turn into Infinity in downstream arithmetic. Commit ad7cc2e.

- [x] CROSS47-seed. Android ticket wizard now accepts and pre-seeds customerId from a nav arg. `Screen.TicketCreate` gained a `createRoute(customerId: Long? = null)` builder and the composable is registered with an optional `customerId` query arg. `TicketCreateViewModel` injects `SavedStateHandle`, reads the arg on init, and a new `setPickedCustomer(id)` helper resolves the row via `CustomerRepository.getCustomer(id).filterNotNull().firstOrNull()` then populates `UiState.selectedCustomer` and advances to the Category step ŌĆö same end-state as tapping a search result. Idempotent: if the user already picked a customer (or walk-in) between launch and the flow completing, the seeder no-ops. Bottom-nav visibility check updated from `== Screen.TicketCreate.route` to `.startsWith(...)` since the registered route template now carries the `?customerId={customerId}` suffix. CustomerDetail's onCreateTicket callback now calls `createRoute(customerId)`. Commit d46d70e.

- [x] CROSS22-badge-cap. Already landed. `DashboardScreen.kt:324` already reads `Text(if (unread > 99) "99+" else unread.toString())` ŌĆö introduced in commit ed9e20b (fix(cross22-badge)), which the original DONETODOS note for CROSS22-badge (line 93) incorrectly described as "no 99+ cap yet". - [x] SEC-M62. `DELETE /tickets/:id` now gated on `requirePermission('tickets.delete')` and hard-blocks when the associated invoice has any `amount_paid > 0`. Prior route was auth-only so any logged-in user could cascade-delete tickets, triggering stock restores and invoice voids. Paid-invoice delete is now rejected regardless of the allow-delete-after-invoice toggle ŌĆö the admin must refund first so the revenue event is debited, not erased. Commit a56e7bb.

- [x] SEC-L39. Recurring appointment auto-generation (`leads.routes.ts:477`) now uses `addMonthsClamped()` that pivots to day-1 before `setMonth` and clamps to the target month's last valid day. Prior `setMonth(getMonth()+i)` silently rolled Jan 31 ŌåÆ Mar 3 on non-leap years (and April 31 ŌåÆ May 1). Weekly/biweekly unchanged ŌĆö `setDate()` already exact across DST for the server's TZ. date-fns not pulled in (would be a new dep) ŌĆö native Date is sufficient for this clamp. Commit 6ede85a.

- [x] SEC-L23. `services/stripe.ts` exports `resetStripeClient()` that sets the module-level `stripeClient` back to null. Any super-admin path that rotates STRIPE_SECRET_KEY at runtime can now call this helper; the next `getStripe()` lazy-inits a fresh client with the new key. Previously the singleton was cached for process lifetime so a rotated key was silently ignored until restart. Commit 761a1ae.

- [x] SEC-L27. Portal `widget.js` now validates `data-server` against a CNAME pattern `https://<sub>.<domain>.<tld>[:port][/path]` (dev exemption for localhost / 127.0.0.1). Prior code accepted any string, so a malicious embedder could point the widget at an attacker-controlled origin and render a lookalike portal to phish customer credentials. Commit a89ff84.

- [x] SEC-L44. 2FA backup codes switched from 32-char hex to 16-char Crockford base32 formatted `XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX` in `auth.routes.ts:780`. Crockford alphabet (0-9 A-Z minus I L O U) excludes confusable pairs so users typing codes off paper don't fat-finger 0/O or 1/l/I. 80 bits of entropy ŌĆö still well above NIST's 10^-6 guess-rate bar for 8 single-use codes. Verify path unchanged (bcrypt.compareSync is format-agnostic); already-enrolled users keep working. Absorbed into commit d46d70e via concurrent-session git interleave (wrong commit message ŌĆö real content change is the Crockford swap in `auth.routes.ts:776-800`).

- [x] SEC-L40. `invoices.routes.ts` payment_plan validator now cross-checks `installments * amount_per Ōēł invoice.total` with tolerance `$0.01 + installments * $0.01` for penny-split rounding. Prior checks validated each field in isolation so 6 ├Ś $10 on a $100 invoice could be saved. Mismatch rejects with 400 and a message showing both sums. Commit fb325aa.

- [x] SEC-L38. Boot-time `import_runs` zombie recovery added to `index.ts` (runs alongside the SMS sweep after `migrateAllTenants()`). Per-tenant UPDATE marks any `import_runs.status IN ('running', 'pending')` as `failed` with `error_log` entry tagged `zombie-recovery: import crashed / server restarted before completion`. Also DELETEs stale `import_locks` rows so new imports can start. Commit b6562fa.

- [x] SEC-L42. `/signup` validation errors ŌĆö malformed email, invalid-format slug, slug-already-taken ŌĆö now all return one generic `Signup failed. Please check your details and try again.` instead of three distinct strings. Prior differences let probes enumerate taken slugs (AZ-042). Validation still runs; specific reason flows to `logger.warn` for operator debugging, never to the wire. Per-email rate limit 429 message unchanged. Commit cf6e581.

- [x] SEC-L29. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` public-route token validators (GET /:token, POST /:token/click, POST /:token/pay) now check `^[A-Za-z0-9_-]{32}$` ŌĆö matching the 24-byte/32-char base64url output of `generateToken()` exactly. Prior `length >= 8` guard let 62^8-space garbage reach the DB lookup. Commit 1d0a0cb.

- [x] CROSS32-ext. - [x] SEC-L33. HTTPS `tlsOptions` now pins a modern AEAD cipher whitelist (`TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384`, `TLS_CHACHA20_POLY1305_SHA256`, `TLS_AES_128_GCM_SHA256`, `ECDHE-ECDSA-AES256-GCM-SHA384`, `ECDHE-RSA-AES256-GCM-SHA384`, ECDHE-*-CHACHA20-POLY1305, ECDHE-*-AES128-GCM-SHA256) and sets `honorCipherOrder: true`. Prior reliance on Node defaults meant a downgrade-happy client could negotiate CBC-mode suites. Commit 9b09a9a.

- [x] SEC-L37. `/sms/send` in `sms.routes.ts:425` now rejects `to` values that don't normalise to 8-15 digits with `Recipient phone is not a valid E.164 number`. Prior code only length-checked `to` (Ōēż30 chars), so "hello", "", emoji, and short digit strings dropped straight through to the provider ŌĆö billable reject + audit noise, and some providers silently swallow malformed destinations into false "delivered" callbacks. Commit 4a3ca61.

- [x] SEC-L35. Boot-time zombie recovery added to `index.ts` (runs once after `migrateAllTenants()`). Per-tenant UPDATE marks any `sms_messages.status = 'sending'` older than 10 minutes as `failed` with tag `zombie-recovery: stuck in sending > 10m after server restart`. Previously stranded rows stayed in 'sending' forever after a crash mid-dispatch, blocking retry UI. Commit 2963767.

- [x] SEC-L36. `sms.routes.ts:543` now awaits `incrementSmsCount(req.tenantId)` inside a try/catch and tags the sms_messages row with `;usage_untracked` on failure. Prior fire-and-forget `.then().catch()` silently skipped the counter on any crash path, letting attackers bypass plan quota via any route that reliably crashed the tracker. Fail-closed here means observable (ops can WHERE-clause the tag) ŌĆö the provider already accepted the send so we can't un-send. Commit 628674d.

- [x] SEC-L31. Outbound webhook HMAC now signs `${timestamp}.${body}` instead of body-only (`services/webhooks.ts:257`). Prior scheme shipped X-Webhook-Timestamp unauthenticated, so a replay attacker could swap the header and fool a freshness-checking receiver into re-accepting a captured body. New scheme binds timestamp into the signed input (Stripe-style). No legacy mode ŌĆö every outbound delivery carries a fresh sig so the cut is clean. Commit baecdd2.

- [x] SEC-L17. Cloudflare DNS retry backoff in `services/cloudflareDns.ts:91` now multiplies the deterministic delay (Retry-After or `base * 2^attempt`) by a random factor in [0.75, 1.25]. Prior purely-exponential backoff caused signup-burst clients to re-fire in lock-step and re-trigger the same 429. Jitter spreads retries across the backoff window. Commit 41657ff.

- [x] SEC-L32. `settings.routes.ts:1860` API-key `bcrypt.hashSync(rawKey, 10)` bumped to cost `12`. API keys carry full tenant scope and skip 2FA ŌĆö at cost 10 (~0.1s/attempt, Node default) the offline brute-force ceiling is 4├Ś weaker than at 12 (~0.4s). Call is once per key creation so user-visible cost is negligible. Commit b62fb4d.

- [x] SEC-L21. `/reports/dashboard` cache key at `reports.routes.ts:34` now `dashboard:${tenantSlug}:${role}` ŌĆö was `dashboard:${tenantSlug}` only. Admin-first-hit no longer poisons the cashier response for the TTL window if any dashboard field is role-gated. Three cache buckets at most (admin/manager/technician) in a typical tenant; acceptable over-cache vs per-user explosion. Commit ea3085a.

- [x] SEC-L20. `catalogScraper.fetchSearchPage` in `services/catalogScraper.ts:390` now caps response body at 10 MiB before `cheerio.load(html)`. Layer 1: reject on `Content-Length > 10 MiB` pre-download. Layer 2: stream-read via `arrayBuffer()` and abort on `byteLength > 10 MiB`. Prior behavior fed arbitrary-size HTML into a synchronous parser, pinning the event loop and ballooning process memory on a malicious / runaway supplier page. Commit f49d746.

- [x] SEC-L19. Backup disk-space pre-check in `services/backup.ts:291` now requires 2├Ś (dbSize + uploadsSize) free ŌĆö prior check only sized the DB. New helper `getDirectorySize()` walks `config.uploadsPath` silently; on sizing failure we fall back to dbSize-only (strictly safer than skipping). Error message splits the estimate so operators can see whether DB or uploads is the bigger consumer. Commit b005bf6.

- [x] SEC-L16. `getOrCreateWebhookSecret` in `services/webhooks.ts:56` rewritten to a race-safe `INSERT OR IGNORE ... VALUES ('webhook_secret', ?)` followed by a SELECT. Prior read ŌåÆ branch ŌåÆ INSERT-or-UPDATE let two concurrent first-time deliveries both generate their own 32-byte secret and race the PRIMARY KEY; loser's outbound payload was already signed with an orphan key the receiver couldn't verify. Atomic now. Commit e1f9591.

- [x] CROSS46. New `util/DateFormatter.kt` (extracted out of `util/Formatters.kt`) exposes two canonical APIs: `formatAbsolute(timestampMs: Long)` ŌåÆ "April 16, 2026" (`LLLL d, yyyy`, locale default), `formatRelative(timestampMs: Long)` ŌåÆ delegated to `android.text.format.DateUtils.getRelativeTimeSpanString` for "just now" / "5 min ago" / "in 2 hr". A companion `formatTimeOfDay(Long)` renders "h:mm a" for Settings-style "April 16, 2026 at 9:17 PM" rendering. - [x] SEC-M18. RMA + loaner list/detail GETs now gated on `requirePermission('inventory.adjust')`. - [x] SEC-M19. `/portal/embed/config` now (a) applies a 60-req / 5-min per-IP `consumeWindowRate` under the new `portal_embed_config` category (429 + Retry-After on over-limit), and (b) returns 404 unless the tenant has opted in via `store_config.portal_embed_enabled = '1'`. Previously the route was wide open and unthrottled ŌĆö attackers could harvest store_name / phone / address / logo across the entire tenant fleet by rotating Host headers. 404 (not 403) when disabled to keep "tenant exists but widget off" indistinguishable from "tenant doesn't exist". Commit bcebe88.

- [x] SEC-M31. `forEachDbAsync` in `index.ts:178` now races every per-tenant callback against a 30s timeout via a `withTimeout` helper. A hung tenant (stuck query, locked WAL, unresponsive file handle) used to stall all subsequent cron work (retention sweeps, appointment reminders, notifications). On timeout the bad tenant's iteration is logged and skipped; the loop proceeds to the next tenant. Iteration remains sequential. Commit 517204e.

- [x] SEC-M27. New `trackInterval` retention cron added to `index.ts` (right after the tenant sweep block) that runs once per UTC day at 03:00 and purges from the MASTER DB: `master_audit_log` older than 730 days, `tenant_auth_events` older than 90 days, `security_alerts` older than 730 days (unacked) / 180 days (acked). Followed by `incremental_vacuum(100)` to return freed pages. Prior state: no retention ŌåÆ these append-only tables grew unbounded (tenant_auth_events especially ŌĆö one row per 2FA prompt). Commit f25a1a2.

- [x] SEC-M33. Credit-note overflow `store_credit_transactions` row (`invoices.routes.ts:891`) now uses `reference_type = 'credit_note_overflow'` instead of the previous `'invoice'`. Reporting/reconciliation tools can now isolate overflow credits from ordinary invoice-to-credit moves. Schema column is free-text `TEXT` so no migration is needed; `reference_id` still points at the source invoice for traceability. Commit 091902b.

- [x] SEC-M23. `recordLockoutFailure` in `utils/rateLimiter.ts:98` rewritten as a single `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT(category, key) DO UPDATE SET count = count + 1` statement. Prior SELECT ŌåÆ branch ŌåÆ INSERT-or-UPDATE pattern raced on concurrent TOTP / login failures: two simultaneous failures could both see row=null and contend on the UNIQUE(category, key) constraint, or the separate UPDATE could lose an increment. Now atomic at the SQL level. Commit 40c6fba.

- [x] SEC-M24. `/auth/change-password` now records the new bcrypt hash into `password_history` and prunes old rows INSIDE the same `adb.transaction([...])` as the user UPDATE + sessions DELETE. Previously the history INSERT happened in a follow-up `adb.run()` call ŌĆö a mid-request crash rotated the password but left history missing, letting the user reuse the new password on next rotation and silently bypass the P2FA8 reuse check. Commit 5406ce0.

- [x] SEC-M30. Per-tenant SQLite `cache_size` dropped from `-64000` (64 MiB) to `-16000` (16 MiB) in `db/tenant-pool.ts:103`. With `MAX_POOL_SIZE=50` the page-cache ceiling goes from 3.2 GiB ŌåÆ ~800 MiB; typical tenant DB (<200 MiB) fits its hot working set in 16 MiB so query latency should not shift. Commit cc5060a.

- [x] SEC-M29. `/health` + `/api/v1/health` now round-trip the master DB via `SELECT 1` and return 503 `{success:false, message:"db unreachable"}` on failure ŌĆö an LB can distinguish "process alive" from "process alive with dead DB handle" (disk full, file locked, pool wedged). `/api/v1/health/ready` additionally round-trips `PRAGMA user_version` on top of the existing `isReady` boot flag so post-boot DB degradation drains the instance instead of serving 500s; `schemaVersion` is now echoed for ops. Commit 1bf3ae5.

- [x] SEC-M22. `GET /super-admin/tenants` list view now destructures `db_path` out of each row before spreading the rest into the response ŌĆö the internal filesystem path (`tenants/<slug>.db`) is no longer echoed to super-admin clients. Single-tenant detail endpoint (`GET /super-admin/tenants/:id`) still carries `db_path` for ops tooling. Commit fac0432.

- [x] CROSS38b. - [x] SEC-H22. `POST /inventory/:id/adjust-stock` (inventory.routes.ts:1076) now role-gates to admin/manager and the UPDATE uses a differential `in_stock = in_stock + ? WHERE id = ? AND in_stock + ? >= 0` + `changes === 0 ŌåÆ 400 Insufficient stock`. Replaces the prior read-check-write race where two parallel `-5` adjustments could both pass the JS precheck. Commit 50a1889.

- [x] SEC-H23. `DELETE /customers/:id` (customers.routes.ts:1222) now requires admin/manager role AND `body.confirm_name` exactly matching `first_name + ' ' + last_name`. Defeats drive-by CSRF and stray mis-click deletes from other tabs ŌĆö the attacker would need the exact name. Existing open-ticket / unpaid-invoice blockers preserved. Cascade-anonymize of sms/FTS/uploads deferred to a follow-up (not blocking this ticket). Commit cfe5635.

- [x] SEC-H26. `POST /invoices/:id/payments` (invoices.routes.ts:377) now rejects with 400 when the request body includes a `customer_id` that does not match `invoice.customer_id`. Body value is validated as a positive integer first. Blocks UI bugs / forged requests that would post a payment against invoice A while declaring customer B (wrong ledger credit). Note spec filename was `pos.routes.ts:249` ŌĆö the actual handler lives in invoices.routes.ts (pos.routes.ts has `POST /transaction` at that line, which is a different surface). Commit 7f06546.

- [x] SEC-H28. `PATCH /refunds/:id/approve` (refunds.routes.ts:165) now wraps the refund status flip + invoice amount_paid decrement in a single `adb.transaction([...])` with `expectChanges: true`. The refund UPDATE carries `WHERE id = ? AND status = 'pending'`; the invoice UPDATE carries `WHERE id = ? AND amount_paid = ?` with the snapshotted prior value. Either guard failing rolls the whole tx back and surfaces a 409. Commission-reversal + store-credit hooks remain post-tx (intentionally best-effort). Commit cb7f2b3.

- [x] SEC-H29. `POST /refunds` (refunds.routes.ts:79) now mounts the shared `idempotent` middleware (short-circuits double-submit within 5 min when `X-Idempotency-Key` is supplied) AND rejects with 403 unless the caller's role is admin or manager. Prevents cashier-tier rubber-stamp requests and the "user clicked Create twice ŌåÆ two pending refund rows" failure mode. Commit bf43cf6.

- [x] SEC-H30. `PATCH /trade-ins/:id` (tradeIns.routes.ts:104) now requires admin/manager role when the requested status is `accepted`, and rejects any `accepted_price` that is not `Number.isFinite && > 0 && <= 100000` (even on non-accepting PATCHes so the field can never be pre-set absurdly low/high). Cap comes from the spec's sanity ceiling. Commit bf39cd2.

- [x] SEC-H31. `POST /rma` (rma.routes.ts:88) and `PATCH /rma/:id/status` (rma.routes.ts:133) both now mount `requirePermission('inventory.edit')`. RMA create/transition is an inventory/supplier-side action, so `inventory.edit` is the closest permission (no dedicated RMA key in PERMISSIONS). Blocks cashier-tier users from queueing fake supplier returns or advancing the state machine to `resolved`. Note spec title said "quick-track" but referenced lines pointed at rma.routes.ts ŌĆö portal's `/quick-track` is a separate unauthenticated public endpoint and out of scope. Commits 2ad3b2d.

Unified the list row to `.uppercase()` so locale-specific divergence (Turkish dotted/dotless i) cannot cause drift between screens. Wired into the DeviceStep chip renderer via `remember(popularDevices)` so it only recomputes when the backing list changes. Lists Ōēż 6 items OR genuinely all-one-brand pass through untouched (no fake mixing when there's only one bucket).

- [x] CROSS25. Removed `data_recovery` + `quick` tiles from `CATEGORY_TILES` in `TicketCreateScreen.kt` ŌĆö neither is a device category. Left an inline comment above the list flagging Data Recovery as a future SERVICE option (surface it on the Service step) and Quick Check-in as a future shortcut flow (ticket-list FAB). `ISSUE_MACROS` entries for both keys retained as harmless fallbacks in case a draft state ever rehydrates with the old category values.

- [x] CROSS18. Root cause was the outer `Scaffold` in `AppNavGraph.kt` passing a `contentWindowInsets` whose top equals the system status bar height. Every child screen's own `Scaffold { topBar = BrandTopAppBar(...) }` also applies the status bar inset inside its `TopAppBar.windowInsets`, so the two stacked ŌĆö hence the ~200px of dead space above "New ticket" / "Dashboard" / "Customers" / "Messages". Fix: `contentWindowInsets = WindowInsets.systemBars.only(Horizontal + Bottom)` on the outer Scaffold so the top inset is owned exclusively by each screen's BrandTopAppBar. TicketCreate/Dashboard/CustomerList/SmsList bodies were already clean (no spurious `padding(top=ŌĆ”)`), so no per-screen edits required.

No bulk-fix needed.

Android sweep handled by CROSS8. Commit bbf4c58.

- [x] CROSS26. Deferred pending an app-wide MaterialIcons family + tint + stroke-weight design decision. - [x] CROSS27-ext. No-op verification: grep for `\u2753` (red question mark) and `\uD83E\uDD14` (thinking face red) across `packages/android/app/src/main/**/*.kt` returned zero hits. CROSS27 (commit cf70508) already covers the only occurrence (TicketCreateScreen "Other" tile swapped to `\u2754`). Nothing to commit.

- [x] SEC-H1. `/reset-password` now wraps the `UPDATE users SET password_hash=ŌĆ”, reset_token=NULL, reset_token_expires=NULL` and the `DELETE FROM sessions WHERE user_id=?` in a single `adb.transaction([ŌĆ”])` call (same pattern as `/change-password` L1585). Previously a crash or connection drop between the two statements could leave a user with a new password but old refresh tokens still live.

- [x] SEC-H5. `/login/2fa-backup` now runs `checkLoginRateLimit(db, ip)` at the top of the handler (mirrors `/login/2fa-verify`) and calls `recordLoginFailure(db, ip)` alongside `recordTotpFailure` on invalid-code paths. Previously only the user-keyed TOTP limiter fired ŌĆö an attacker enumerating `challengeToken`s could spray backup-code guesses across many users from a single IP and never trip a single limiter.

- [x] SEC-H7. `/forgot-password` builds the reset URL from `config.baseDomain` (prefixed with `tenantSlug.` when multi-tenant) instead of `req.headers.host`. A malicious Host / X-Forwarded-Host header previously let an attacker coerce the server into minting a reset link pointing at their own domain and emailing it to the real user ŌĆö a one-click credential harvester. `https://` is now hard-coded; the old `req.secure` branch is gone because password reset must never go over plaintext HTTP.

- [x] SEC-H8. `/account/2fa/disable` now runs `DELETE FROM sessions WHERE user_id=? AND id != ?` (preserving the caller's current session) and `res.clearCookie('deviceTrust', ŌĆ”)` after successfully wiping `totp_secret` / `totp_enabled`. Previously any other logged-in session and the browser-side "remember this device" JWT would silently survive a self-service 2FA disable, so a compromised cookie from a pre-disable state could keep reading the account without another login.

- [x] SEC-H9. `/login/set-password` scopes the password-setup UPDATE with `AND password_set = 0` and returns a generic 401 when `changes === 0`. A race ŌĆö or any future bug that hands out two valid challenges for the same user ŌĆö can no longer overwrite a password that has already been set. The challenge token is still consumed on entry; this guard is defence-in-depth in case a challenge issued during first-run is replayed against an account that has since completed setup.

- [x] SEC-H10. Successful `/login/2fa-verify` and `/login/2fa-backup` flows now call `clearRateLimit(db, 'login_ip', ip)` and `clearRateLimit(db, 'login_user', '${tenantSlug}:${username}')` after 2FA completes (in addition to the existing TOTP counter clear). Previously the password-stage IP and user counters stayed populated even after a legitimate 2FA success, so an attacker who had already spent 9 bad-password attempts against a known username could leave that user one bad attempt away from the 30-minute user-level lockout ŌĆö a cheap DoS against the real account owner.

- [x] SEC-H12. `/auth/refresh` now asserts `payload.tenantSlug === req.tenantSlug` using `crypto.timingSafeEqual` on equal-length utf-8 buffers (with `null` normalized to `''`) immediately after the JWT signature + `type === 'refresh'` check. A valid refresh token issued for tenant-a can no longer be replayed on tenant-b; both tenants share the same `jwtRefreshSecret`, so signature alone wasn't sufficient isolation. Mismatch returns a generic 401.

- [x] SEC-M9. Refresh rotation now preserves the original lifetime category by deriving `(payload.exp - payload.iat)` from the incoming refresh token (clamped to `[1h, 90d]`) and re-using that value for both the new JWT's `expiresIn` and the cookie `maxAge`. Previously the handler hard-coded 30d, which silently shortened trustDevice (90d) sessions on every refresh. The clamp prevents forged tokens with bogus exp/iat from minting absurd lifetimes.

- [x] SEC-M10. `/auth/refresh` now wraps every exit with `audit(db, 'refresh_failed' | 'refresh_success', ŌĆ”)` + `logTenantAuthEvent(...)`. Tracked reasons: `missing_token`, `wrong_type`, `tenant_mismatch`, `session_expired`, `idle_timeout`, `user_missing_or_inactive`, `verify_error` (catch block includes JS error name). Successful rotation logs `refresh_success` with the sessionId. Without this, a stolen refresh token could rotate indefinitely with zero trace in the audit log.

- [x] SEC-M11. `/auth/refresh` now `DELETE FROM sessions WHERE id = ?` before the 401 when the user lookup returns `is_active = 0` or row-not-found. Orphaned session rows previously survived user deactivation; if the same user id were later re-activated, the stale session row would silently become valid again. This also prevents the session table from accumulating dead rows tied to deactivated accounts.

- [x] SEC-M12. `/auth/change-password` UPDATE now includes `reset_token = NULL, reset_token_expires = NULL` alongside `password_hash`/`password_set`. A pending password-reset token that was outstanding when the user changed their password previously remained valid until expiry ŌĆö giving an attacker with a phished reset link the ability to set the password back after the legitimate owner rotated it. Change-password now invalidates any such pending token in the same atomic transaction as the password update + session revoke.

### Production readiness audit batch 2 (PROD18-20, 22-28, 30, 42-45) ŌĆö verification only

- [x] PROD18. Cross-tenant read audit ŌĆö the tenant isolation model is *physical*, not row-level: `packages/server/src/middleware/tenantResolver.ts:420` sets `req.db = getTenantDb(tenant.slug)` which opens `{tenantDataDir}/{slug}.db` (a separate SQLite file per tenant), so any tenant-scoped route issuing `WHERE id = ?` is already scoped to that tenant's file. Cross-tenant exposure is only possible from routes that touch the master DB directly ŌĆö those are isolated to `super-admin.routes.ts`, `master-admin.routes.ts`, `management.routes.ts` (localhost-only), plus the tier-gate blocks in `tickets.routes.ts`/`pos.routes.ts`/`estimates.routes.ts`/`leads.routes.ts`/`voice.routes.ts` which only read/write `tenant_usage` scoped to `req.tenantId`. No tenant-scoped route reads cross-tenant rows from master DB.

- [x] PROD19. Template-string interpolation audit ŌĆö five call sites grep'd across `packages/server/src` that interpolate into `db.prepare(\`...${...}...\`)`. All five are safe: (1) `master-admin.routes.ts:325` + `super-admin.routes.ts:752,825` interpolate column names built from a hardcoded `MASTER_TENANT_UPDATE_WHITELIST` / `TENANT_UPDATE_FIELD_WHITELIST` set with an explicit whitelist-bypass guard one line above; (2) `super-admin.routes.ts:1301,1381` interpolate a `WHERE` clause composed from `conditions.join(' AND ')` where every condition is a hardcoded fragment (`severity = ?`, `tenant_slug = ?`, `ip_address = ?`, `event = ?`). Values come through `?` placeholders. No user-controlled data reaches SQL. Same grep on `packages/server/src/services` returns `repairDeskImport.ts` `DROP TRIGGER`/`DELETE FROM` interpolations over a hardcoded `table`/`column` list (migration helper, not a request handler), `tenant-provisioning.ts:106,845` interpolating `UNAVAILABLE_STATUSES`/`where` built from constants.

- [x] PROD20. `db.exec(...)` audit ŌĆö every call site (`db/master-connection.ts`, `db/migrate.ts`, `db/migrate-all-tenants.ts`, `services/metricsCollector.ts`, `services/stripe.ts`, `services/tenant-provisioning.ts`, `services/tenant-repair.ts`, `services/repairDeskImport.ts`) receives either (a) a hardcoded SQL literal or (b) `sql = fs.readFileSync(migrationFile)` from `packages/server/src/db/migrations/` (filesystem, not request body). None receive user input.

- [x] PROD21. Deep-audit dynamic-WHERE routes ŌĆö audited `search.routes.ts`, `import.routes.ts`, `reports.routes.ts`, `customers.routes.ts`. **No exploitable violations.** Every dynamic `WHERE`/`ORDER BY`/`LIMIT` constructor pulls column names from a static whitelist and binds values via `?` placeholders. Hardened the following defense-in-depth sites: (1) `reports.routes.ts` ŌĆö `LIMIT ${dailySalesLimit}` / `LIMIT ${openTicketsLimit}` / `LIMIT ${limit}` (dashboard-kpis + parts-usage) now bind via `?` instead of splicing server-chosen ints; (2) `reports.routes.ts` tech-leaderboard ŌĆö `sinceClause` (one of three hard-coded DATE() literals) replaced with `DATE('now', ?)` + bound `sinceModifier`; (3) `reports.routes.ts` day-of-week-profit ŌĆö inline `${tzModifier(tz)}` splice replaced with `?`-bound parameter (matches the existing hour-of-day / tech-suggestion pattern at lines 2086, 2552). (4) Added `PROD21:` explanatory comments on the allow-lists that still splice column names: `customers.routes.ts` `allowedSorts` (sort columns), `customers.routes.ts` `CUSTOMER_COLUMNS` loop (PATCH SET clause), `reports.routes.ts` presets `updates[]` (all pushed strings are hard-coded literals). `search.routes.ts` was already clean ŌĆö FTS MATCH terms are sanitized by `ftsMatchExpr()` (200-char cap, alphanumeric + whitespace only, 16-token limit) and every LIKE/MATCH value binds via `?`. `import.routes.ts` has zero dynamic WHERE construction ŌĆö all SQL is hardcoded with `?` placeholders. `customers.routes.ts` bulk ops (GDPR-erase, export, communications) generate `IN (${placeholders})` strings from `.map(() => '?').join()` with the value array passed via spread, never from user input. Build: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean.

- [x] PROD22. Validation library ŌĆö `zod: ^3.24.0` is declared in `packages/shared/package.json:24` but no `import { z } from 'zod'` exists anywhere in `packages/server/src` or `packages/shared/src`. The live validation stack is the custom `packages/server/src/utils/validate.ts` (exports `validateEmail`, `validatePhoneDigits`, `validateHexColor`, `validateRequiredString`, etc.) plus ad-hoc `String()`/`parseInt()` checks. **Gap flagged** ŌĆö Zod is installed but unused; Phase 3.2 schema-validation work still needs to be done. `packages/shared/src/validators/` directory exists but is empty.

- [x] PROD23. Schema validation spot-check on 3 high-risk routes ŌĆö none of them use Zod `.parse(req.body)`. `signup.routes.ts:296-307` uses `validateEmail`/`validateRequiredString`/`validateSlug` helpers (custom functions, not schema-based). `billing.routes.ts` has no per-request body validation but the Checkout session is built from `req.tenantId`/`req.tenantSlug`/DB-retrieved admin email (no user input reaches Stripe) and the webhook path calls `verifyWebhook(req.body, sig)` before any processing. `settings.routes.ts:244-254` uses `validateRequiredString`/`validateEmail`/`validatePhoneDigits` per field. **Gap flagged** ŌĆö no Zod schemas on any of the three; follow-up schema work required (tracked by PROD22 gap).

- [x] PROD24. Multer `limits.fileSize` ŌĆö all six `multer()` instances under `packages/server/src` have `limits.fileSize` set: `bench.routes.ts:114` (5MB), `inventory.routes.ts:50` (5MB), `inventoryEnrich.routes.ts:92` (5MB), `settings.routes.ts:76` (5MB), `tickets.routes.ts:59` (10MB), `sms.routes.ts:51` (MMS_MAX_SIZE constant). No missing caps.

- [x] PROD25. Uploads serving ŌĆö `packages/server/src/index.ts:868-887` wraps the `/uploads` mount in a custom handler that (a) decodes and rejects any path containing `..` or `\\`, (b) computes `basePath = path.join(config.uploadsPath, req.tenantSlug)` so each tenant only sees its own folder, (c) re-resolves the final path and checks `resolved.startsWith(path.resolve(basePath))` to block traversal, (d) then hands off to `express.static(basePath, { dotfiles: 'deny', index: false })`. Not raw filesystem.

- [x] PROD26. `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` audit ŌĆö only one live usage across `packages/web/src`: `pages/tickets/TicketNotes.tsx:323` and it is wrapped in `DOMPurify.sanitize(event.description || '', { ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b','i','em','strong'], ALLOWED_ATTR: [] })`. `pages/print/PrintPage.tsx:930` only mentions `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` inside a comment explaining why a `<style>` child was used instead. SA4-1 left-overs are clean.

- [x] PROD27. Email/SMS template escaping ŌĆö `services/notifications.ts:438-461` builds per-variable HTML-escaped vars via `escapeHtml(...)` before `.replace(/\{customer_name\}/g, htmlVars.customer_name)` substitution, so customer-controlled strings cannot break out of email HTML. SMS path at `notifications.ts:378-382` uses the raw `smsVars` (correct ŌĆö SMS is plain text, HTML escaping would corrupt the message). `routes/sms.routes.ts:107` `substituteVars` also uses plain `replace`, plain-text context.

- [x] PROD28. Path traversal grep ŌĆö only one match for `path.join(.*req\.` in `packages/server/src`: `index.ts:876` (`path.join(config.uploadsPath, req.tenantSlug)`). `req.tenantSlug` is validated against `/^[a-z0-9]([a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?$/` by `tenantResolver.ts:361` before it's set on the request, and the join is immediately followed by the `.startsWith(path.resolve(basePath))` traversal guard. No `path.join` using `req.params`/`req.query`/`req.body` found.

- [x] PROD30. Open-redirect audit ŌĆö only two `res.redirect` call sites exist: (1) `index.ts:572` redirects HTTPŌåÆHTTPS using `sanitizeRedirectHost(req.headers.host)` + `sanitizeRedirectUrl(req.url)` (SEC-H5 CRLF-injection hardening), no `next`/`returnUrl` accepted; (2) `routes/voice.routes.ts:198` redirects to `call.recording_url` which is populated by the voice-provider webhook (not user-supplied). No routes accept a `next`/`returnUrl`/`redirect` query or body parameter.

- [x] PROD42. Per-tenant SQLite isolation ŌĆö `db/tenant-pool.ts:86` builds the DB path as `path.join(config.tenantDataDir, \`${slug}.db\`)` where `config.tenantDataDir = packages/server/data/tenants/`. `config` at `config.ts:106` resolves this once at boot. After the file is opened, `tenant-pool.ts:94-97` re-resolves the path and rejects anything that doesn't `startsWith(path.resolve(config.tenantDataDir))`. Pool caches up to 50 connections, evicts LRU on overflow, health-checks every 30s. One file per tenant; cross-tenant reads are impossible at the DB layer.

- [x] PROD43. `tenantResolver` fails closed ŌĆö every unresolved/invalid tenant path returns an explicit `res.status(404).json(...)` + `return`: lines 289 (bogus Host), 343 (bare-domain API hit), 362 (bad slug format), 368 (reserved subdomain), 390 (tenant row not found), 396 (suspended), 409 (unknown status). The `provisioning` branch at line 403 returns a distinct 503 ŌĆö legitimate transient state. No silent fallthrough paths.

- [x] PROD44. Super-admin separate auth ŌĆö `routes/super-admin.routes.ts:465` mounts `router.use(superAdminAuth)` which at line 174 verifies a JWT signed with `config.superAdminSecret` (distinct from the tenant JWT secret) using pinned `algorithms: ['HS256']`, `issuer: 'bizarre-crm'`, `audience: 'bizarre-crm-super-admin'`, then validates the session row in the master DB's `super_admin_sessions` table. Not the tenant `authMiddleware`. The sibling `masterAuthMiddleware` in `middleware/masterAuth.ts` uses the same pinned options for any routes that import it. `master-admin.routes.ts:38-43` is additionally hardened with a kill switch (`MASTER_ADMIN_LEGACY_ENABLED` env var) returning 410 unless explicitly enabled ŌĆö the router is no longer mounted in `index.ts`.

- [x] PROD45. Tenant code ŌåÆ master DB writes ŌĆö `grep -rn 'masterDb.*\.run\(' packages/server/src/routes` returns only `super-admin.routes.ts`, `master-admin.routes.ts` (disabled, see PROD44), and `management.routes.ts` (localhost-only per lines 1-9). Tenant-scoped route handlers (`tickets.routes.ts:874,3706`, `pos.routes.ts:1007`, `estimates.routes.ts:336,673`, `leads.routes.ts:863`, `voice.routes.ts:389`) also touch `masterDb`, but every write is scoped to `tenant_usage` with the current tenant's id (`tierReservationTenantId`/`warrantyTenantId = req.tenantId`) for tier-gate counters ŌĆö not a cross-tenant write. No tenant code issues `INSERT`/`UPDATE`/`DELETE` against another tenant's data in master DB.

## 2026-04-16

### Server security fixes batch (SEC-M14, M15, M25, M42, L2, L8, L24)

- [x] SEC-M14. `deposits.routes.ts` `POST /` now calls `requireManagerOrAdmin(req)` at the top of the handler (mirrors the existing gate on `POST /:id/apply-to-invoice` + `POST /:id/refund` in the same file). Collecting a deposit moves money; allowing any authenticated tenant user to create one was inconsistent with the rest of the money-movement handlers. Commit bf4520f.

- [x] SEC-M15. `signup.routes.ts` adds a per-email in-memory rate-limit Map (`signupEmailCounters`, 3 attempts per normalized-lowercase email per hour) enforced after email-format validation so invalid addresses can't burn quota slots. Stale entries are swept every 5 min on the same cadence as the existing `pendingSignups` sweeper. The existing per-IP signupLimiter remains; the new layer catches rotating-IP attacks targeting a single victim email. Commit 5e6377a.

- [x] SEC-M25. `services/stripe.ts` `handleWebhookEvent` catch block now `DELETE FROM stripe_webhook_events WHERE stripe_event_id = ?` before re-throwing, so a handler exception releases the `INSERT OR IGNORE` idempotency claim and Stripe's retry (triggered by the now-propagated 400 at `billing.routes.ts` webhookHandler) can re-drive the event. Previously the claim persisted + the outer route returned 200 `{received:true}`, so a single transient failure silently dropped the event forever. Commit af96996.

- [x] SEC-M42. `services/blockchyp.ts` exports `sweepStuckPaymentIdempotency(db)` ŌĆö flips `payment_idempotency` rows stuck in `pending` for >5 min to `failed` with a janitor error_message. `index.ts` registers a `trackInterval` every 5 min that iterates tenant DBs via `forEachDb` and invokes the sweeper per tenant. Swallows "no such table" for tenants on pre-080 schema; logs other errors. Without this, a server crash between INSERT and the BlockChyp-response UPDATE leaves the `(invoice_id, client_request_id)` UNIQUE key locked forever ŌĆö legitimate retries hit 409 permanently. Commit 7f5807e.

- [x] SEC-L2. `portal.routes.ts` introduces `NORMALIZED_DIGITS_EXPR(column)` ŌĆö a SQL expression that strips punctuation (`-`, ` `, `(`, `)`, `+`, `.`, `/`) then drops the leading `1` for 11-digit US numbers, mirroring `normalizePhone()`. The two portal lookups (`POST /login` and `POST /register/send-code`, across `customers.phone`, `customers.mobile`, and `customer_phones.phone`) now compare with `=` instead of `LIKE '%<normalized>'`. Suffix matching previously let any stored number whose trailing digits matched authenticate a different customer (e.g. "9995551234567" colliding with "5551234567"). Commit c8b7de6.

- [x] SEC-L8. Root + server `package.json` engine ranges tightened from `>=22.0.0 <25` to `>=22.11.0 <23` (Node 22 LTS). Added `.npmrc` with `engine-strict=true` so `npm install` hard-fails on a non-conforming Node instead of warning. Local dev confirmed on v22.15.0. Commit 8da2c53.

- [x] SEC-L24. `index.ts` wraps `GET /api/v1/info` with a new `infoAuthGate` middleware: in `config.multiTenant` mode the endpoint now runs through `authMiddleware` (401 without a valid Bearer + tenant-match). In single-tenant mode the endpoint remains public so the Android app's QR bootstrap flow keeps working. Previously the endpoint leaked LAN IP + server URL to any unauthenticated caller ŌĆö verified live on Tailscale per LIVE-08. Commit ebbc2ed.

### Production readiness audit batch (PROD49-51, 62 re-verify, 71-76)

- [x] PROD49. No body logging in route handlers. `Grep 'console\.(log|info|debug|warn|error).*req\.body|logger\.(info|debug).*body:'` across `packages/server/src/routes` returns zero matches. Normal `req.body` usage is strictly destructuring for validation, not logging.

- [x] PROD50. `services/crashTracker.ts` persists `CrashEntry = { id, timestamp, route, errorMessage, errorStack, type, recovered }` to `data/crash-log.json`. No request body, headers, query, or params are captured. `redactSecrets()` further scrubs the error message/stack for bearer tokens, JWTs, query credentials, and Twilio SIDs before write. Safe.

- [x] PROD51. Most `res.status(403)` sites in `packages/server/src/routes` are role/permission gates (admin / manager / super-admin), tier-upgrade gates (`upgrade_required`), or signature verification failures (`'Invalid signature'`) ŌĆö none of these should be 404. FINDING for future work: `portal-enrich.routes.ts:114` returns 403 on `req.portalTicketId !== ticketId` ("Access restricted to your tracked ticket") and `portal-enrich.routes.ts:134` returns 403 on `req.portalCustomerId !== customerId` ŌĆö both confirm resource existence to an unauthorized portal caller. Low-priority enumeration vector, but violates the "indistinguishable from not-found" principle. Tracked as a follow-up audit entry.

- [x] PROD62 (re-verify). `package-lock.json` is tracked in git at the repo root (`git ls-files package-lock.json` returns one hit). File present, 444KB, dated 2026-04-14. Still committed as required.

FINDING: the canonical `NODE_ENV=production` deploy note remains documented only in `setup.bat` / env setup; README does not restate it. Low-priority doc gap ŌĆö users deploying from source don't have a single-line sanity check.

- [x] PROD72. Three `NODE_ENV !== 'production'` sites found; zero `NODE_ENV === 'development'` sites. All reviewed: (a) `middleware/tenantResolver.ts:44` and `:297` ŌĆö accept bare IPv4 hosts and route to `DEV_TENANT_SLUG` so Android-on-LAN works without DNS. Comment-documented as dev-only. (b) `middleware/errorHandler.ts:19` ŌĆö logs `err.stack` to stderr only outside prod. Client response never includes stack regardless of env. None expose routes or relax auth in production.

- [x] PROD73. `scripts/repair-tenant.ts` grepped for `DROP TABLE|DELETE FROM` (case-insensitive) returns zero matches. Safe ŌĆö no destructive DDL/DML. The script only creates/repairs missing admin users, upload dirs, CF records, and schema, consistent with the MEMORY rule "Tenant DB files are sacred."

- [x] PROD74. `db/migrate.ts:8-33` creates `_migrations (name TEXT UNIQUE, applied_at)` on first run, loads applied names into a Set, and `if (applied.has(file)) continue;` skips before re-exec. Each successful exec is followed by `INSERT INTO _migrations (name) VALUES (?)` inside the same transaction (or `@no-transaction` header for schema-toggling migrations). Idempotent by construction.

- [x] PROD75. Grep for `DROP TABLE|TRUNCATE|DELETE FROM` across `packages/server/src/db/migrations/*.sql` returns 7 files: 004/008/042 (FTS/ticket_notes rebuild with `IF EXISTS` guards), 009 (status cleanup guarded by `WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT status_id FROM tickets ...) AND id NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT status_id FROM ticket_devices ...)`), 013 (invoices rebuild: temp table ŌåÆ copy ŌåÆ DROP ŌåÆ rename, all inside migration transaction), 097/098 (DELETE FROMs are AFTER-DELETE trigger bodies scoped by `WHERE ... = OLD.id`, not one-shot migrations). All have adequate guards. No unguarded mass deletions.

- [x] PROD76. `ls packages/server/src/db/migrations | sort | awk -F_ '{print $1}' | uniq -d` reports TWO prefix collisions: `049` has three files (`049_customer_is_active.sql`, `049_po_status_workflow.sql`, `049_sms_scheduled_and_archival.sql`) and `050` has two (`050_appointment_ticket_id.sql`, `050_leads_estimates_automation.sql`). `migrate.ts:26` sorts by full filename so order is still deterministic lexically; the files are effectively applied in the order shown above. FINDING: the prefix is no longer unique ŌĆö any future migration keyed on "049" is ambiguous. Renumbering would require a coordinated DB edit and is higher-risk than the status quo; flagged for visibility but not actioned.

VM exposes `isEffectivelyOnline`; the bottom-bar Print control disables the `TextButton` when either guard fails, and a wrapping `Box` surfaces a "Print requires network + configured server" toast when the user taps while disabled. List screens + the detail's Room flow see the correct `amount_due`/`status` immediately instead of waiting for a separate refresh. `refreshInvoiceDetailInBackground` delegates to the same helper.

    - Opinion strings about people/customers/competitors: **0 hits**. Every grep match for `stupid`/`dumb`/`worst`/`garbage`/`ripoff`/`useless`/`broken` is a technical usage (`"worst case"`, `"garbage input"`, `"DUMB component"` architectural term, `"broken" ticket status`, `"useless for staffing decisions"` re: date math, the `ANGRY_WORDS` sentiment lexicon for inbox triage). References to `RepairDesk` are factual/technical only (`"RepairDesk's public API"`, `"RD typo field: hostory"`, etc.) ŌĆö CLAUDE.md explicitly notes RD ships misspelled field names, so these comments are documenting real API quirks, not opinions.
    - Brand / product identifiers `bizarreelectronics` / `bizarre-crm` / `Bizarre Electronics`: intentional product/tenant/bundle naming per user decision rule ŌĆö kept. Includes Android `com.bizarreelectronics.crm`, iOS `com.bizarreelectronics.crm`, `electron-builder.yml appId`, `scripts/repair-tenant.ts` example-slug, vite dev-proxy `Host: bizarreelectronics.bizarrecrm.com`, landing page `bizarreelectronics.com` reference. All legit.
    - RepairDesk account IDs: **0 hits**. `RD_API_KEY` is env var name only; placeholder account_id `'1234567'` is a provider-config UI placeholder.
    - Phone numbers: `9709143026` removed from DONETODOS.md. All `555-01xx` placeholders in UI (`CustomerCreatePage`, `PortalLogin`, `CommunicationPage`, `QuickSmsModal`, etc.) use the NANPA-reserved fictional-use range ŌĆö legitimate.
    - PROD91 sampleData.ts verification: confirmed **100% synthetic**. 5 hardcoded seed customers (Alex Demo / Jamie Sample / Robin Test / Morgan Example / Casey Preview) with `@example.com` RFC-2606 reserved-domain emails and `303-555-01xx` NANPA fictional-use phones. 10 hardcoded generic device repair entries (no real customer order history). Every row is tagged `[Sample]` for removability. No JSON import, no RepairDesk dump, no real-customer leakage.
  Build smoke: `cd packages/web && npm run build` clean (8.40s, all assets emitted). `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Commit: see `chore(prod85-87-89-91)`.

- [x] SEC-L4. Bumped `LOGIN_MIN_DURATION_MS` from 100ms to 250ms in `auth.routes.ts:26` ŌĆö equalizes wall-clock response time so valid-user vs invalid-user branches converge further under realistic load.

- [x] SEC-L25. Explicit `app.disable('x-powered-by')` before `helmet()` call in `index.ts:594`. Helmet already strips this header, but the explicit disable documents intent and survives future helmet config regressions.

- [x] SEC-M3. Super-admin TOTP verify replaces the hand-rolled `otp === code` string comparison with `otplib.verifySync({ token, secret, epochTolerance: 30 })` in `super-admin.routes.ts:406-416`. otplib uses constant-time comparison internally; the same ┬▒30s (┬▒1 step) clock-skew tolerance is preserved. Removes a user-supplied-string vs derived-secret timing oracle on the 2FA path.

- [x] SEC-L30. Vonage SMS provider default signer is `sha256hmac` (was already set in `vonage.ts:66`; corrected the stale default annotation in `providers/sms/types.ts:145` which still claimed `md5hash` and added a SEC-L30 comment at the constructor). Legacy md5hmac / md5hash variants are still accepted for tenants whose Vonage dashboard is configured that way, but new installs get sha256hmac.

The `/api/v1` cache-control middleware in `index.ts` now emits `private, no-store, max-age=0` for PII paths (`/api/v1/customers/*`, `/api/v1/tickets/*`, `/api/v1/invoices/*`, `/api/v1/auth/me`) on every method, and keeps the existing `private, no-cache` on GETs elsewhere.
